\subparagraph{\texorpdfstring{§4.47.37.2 --- Cognitive-channel
finite-buffer numerical optimum (\texttt{exp157} / H102 / O13 / PARTIAL
3/5)}{§4.47.37.2 --- Cognitive-channel finite-buffer numerical optimum (exp157 / H102 / O13 / PARTIAL 3/5)}}\label{cognitive-channel-finite-buffer-numerical-optimum-exp157-h102-o13-partial-35}

V3.21 §4.47.36.4 left an open question: \emph{why} does the empirical
MAXENT-derived β across 11 corpora cluster near 1.5? V3.21 was honest
that this is a \textbf{structural-empirical} observation, not a
deductive cognitive derivation. The V3.21 §4.47.36.5 ``future paths''
listed three candidate routes (Tsallis, drift-diffusion, Miller 1956
working-memory) without committing to any of them.

\texttt{exp157\_beta\_from\_cognitive\_channel} (PREREG hash
\texttt{ba78303a4e83c43a525195955e6deacd4077a98a21f794b170c2b02856ee778c},
H102) pre-registers and tests the \textbf{Miller 1956 finite-buffer
route} numerically. The protocol:

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{Route A} (anchor, no recomputation): the V3.20 LOO modal β =
  \textbf{1.50} is cited as a fixed reference value.
\item
  \textbf{Route B} (numerical, NEW): for a candidate β, find the MAXENT
  distribution \texttt{p\_k\ ∝\ exp(−μ\ k\^{}β)\ /\ Z} whose
  \textbf{buffer leak}
  \texttt{L\_B\ =\ Σ\_\{k\ \textgreater{}\ B\}\ p\_k} equals a target ε
  (Miller's 7±2 working-memory loss tolerance). The cognitive-channel
  optimum is the β at which the resulting \texttt{p\_max\ =\ p\_1}
  matches the V3.21 pool-median p\_max = 0.2857. Operating-point grid:
  \texttt{(B,\ ε)\ ∈\ \{5,\ 7,\ 9\}\ ×\ \{0.01,\ 0.05,\ 0.10\}} (Miller
  7±2 explicitly + leak tightness sensitivity).
\item
  \textbf{Route C} (regression, NEW): linear regression
  \texttt{β\_c\ =\ a\ +\ b\ ·\ log(p\_max(c))} on the 11 V3.21 (β\_c,
  p\_max(c)) pairs, evaluated at the pool log-median.
\end{enumerate}

\textbf{Pre-registered verdict ladder} (5 criteria, strict counting):

  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\linewidth - 4\tabcolsep) * \real{0.3333}}@{}}
\toprule\noalign{}
\begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright

\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright

\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright

\end{minipage} \\

\bottomrule\noalign{}

\textbf{C1} numerical convergence (constraints to 1e-6, brentq vs
bisection drift \textless{} 1e-6) & \textbf{PASS} & p\_max drift =
1.3e-12, leak drift = 2.8e-17, μ drift = 2.8e-17 \\
\textbf{C2} Route B central β\_opt (B=7, ε=0.05) ∈ {[}1.3, 1.7{]} &

slope \textgreater{} 0 & \textbf{FAIL} & R² = \textbf{0.297} (slope =
+0.65, intercept-at-median = 1.51 ✓; only R² fails) \\
\textbf{C5} 3-way pairwise agreement \textbar Δ\textbar{} ≤ 0.20 &
\textbf{PASS} & max diff = \textbf{0.117} (V3.20 anchor 1.50 vs Route B
1.40 vs Route C 1.51) \\
\end{longtable}
}

\textbf{Verdict: \texttt{PARTIAL\_F75\_beta\_cognitive\_directional} (3
/ 5 PASS).} Receipt:
\texttt{results/experiments/exp157\_beta\_from\_cognitive\_channel/exp157\_beta\_from\_cognitive\_channel.json}.
Tier-C observation O13 added.

\textbf{What this establishes (and what it does not).}

\emph{Establishes}: at Miller's central operating point (B = 7, ε =
0.05), under MAXENT with finite-buffer regularisation, the β at which
the resulting distribution's \texttt{p\_max} matches the V3.21
pool-median is \textbf{β = 1.3955} --- within \texttt{0.10} of the V3.20
LOO modal β = 1.50, within \texttt{0.12} of the Route C log-regression
intercept = 1.5125, and within the \texttt{0.20} 3-way agreement
tolerance. This is \textbf{the first numerical demonstration that β ≈
1.5 emerges from a cognitive-channel constraint} (Miller 7±2
working-memory finite buffer), not just from data-fitting.

\emph{Does not establish}: a universal constant β = 3/2. The 9-cell
sensitivity grid (\texttt{exp157} Route B) shows β\_opt varies from 0.66
(loose buffer: B=9, ε=0.10) to 3.50 (tight buffer: B=5, ε=0.01) ---
i.e., the cognitive optimum is \textbf{strongly dependent on the
working-memory parameters} within Miller's published 7±2 envelope. Route
C's R² = 0.297 also indicates that \textbf{per-corpus β is not fully
predicted by p\_max alone}: Pāli (β = 0.97, p\_max = 0.48) and Quran (β
= 2.53, p\_max = 0.73) both deviate from the regression line in
different directions, reflecting genuine rhyme-design heterogeneity
(\texttt{exp156} cognitive-channel partition: super-Gaussian /
Weibull-1.5 / near-exponential).

The honest summary: \textbf{β = 1.5 is the central tendency of
cognitive-channel feasible MAXENT distributions at Miller's 7±2
mid-point}, with per-corpus variation reflecting authentic differences
in rhyme-concentration design within the same general framework. F75's
V3.18 PARTIAL, V3.19 PARTIAL+, V3.20 STRONG, V3.21 STRONG, and V3.22
directional cognitive-channel support all coexist on the historical
record without retraction.

\subparagraph{§4.47.37.4 --- Honest scope after
V3.22}\label{honest-scope-after-v3.22}

\textbf{What V3.22 DOES claim}:

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  F-Universal is an \textbf{exact algebraic re-statement} of F75 in
  dimensionless Rényi-gap form (proven to machine epsilon in V3.18
  §4.47.33.1; restated in V3.22 with explicit notation).
\item
  The Miller 1956 finite-buffer cognitive-channel optimum at the
  \textbf{central} operating point (B = 7, ε = 0.05, target =
  pool-median p\_max) is \textbf{β = 1.3955}, within 3-way agreement
  tolerance of both the V3.20 LOO modal β = 1.50 and the Route C
  empirical regression intercept = 1.5125.
\item
  F-Universal absorbs F79 as the corollary ``Quran's H\_EL is the lowest
  of the 11 corpora'', under the universal 1-bit Shannon--Rényi gap.
\item
  The \texttt{exp157} PARTIAL verdict (3/5 PASS) provides
  \textbf{directional} cognitive-channel support for β ≈ 1.5, NOT a
  deductive theorem.
\end{itemize}

\textbf{What V3.22 does NOT claim}:

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  A deductive derivation of β = 3/2 as a universal constant. The 9-cell
  Miller 7±2 sensitivity grid shows β\_opt ∈ {[}0.66, 3.50{]} across the
  published Miller envelope; only the central operating point sits in
  the tight band {[}1.3, 1.7{]}.
\item
  An extension of F75 / F-Universal beyond 11 alphabetic-script corpora.
  Cross-tradition-pool extension to Classical Chinese (Daodejing, see
  §4.47.38 below --- \texttt{exp158}
  \texttt{DIRECTIONAL\_F\_UNIVERSAL\_LARGER\_GAP\_FOR\_LOGOGRAPHIC},
  \textbf{0/3 narrow-band, 1/3 widened-band}) is reported as a
  directional logographic-script disclosure, not a cleanly-extending
  universal. Gating to N = 22 (CRITICAL-1) remains blocked on data
  acquisition for the remaining cross-tradition pool.
\item
  Any change to F75's V3.20 STRONG / V3.21 STRONG locked PASS status.
  F75 is still F75. F-Universal is its alias, not its replacement.
\item
  A retraction of V3.21's H101 STRONG verdict, V3.20's H100 STRONG
  verdict, V3.19's FN27 (PARTIAL+ on H99, the Pearson-r fit-tightness
  paradox), or V3.18's FN26 (PARTIAL on H98, the C2 monotonicity
  partial-fail).
\end{itemize}

\textbf{No locked PASS finding's status changes}. F-Universal is a
labelling alias added to F75's row in \texttt{RANKED\_FINDINGS.md} and
\texttt{KEY\_FINDINGS.md}. The Tier-C observation count goes 12 → 14
across the V3.22 sprint as a whole (O13: cognitive-channel finite-buffer
directional support from \texttt{exp157}; O13b:
logographic-script-boundary scope disclosure from \texttt{exp158}, see
§4.47.38 below).

\paragraph{\texorpdfstring{§4.47.38 --- V3.22: F-Universal
logographic-script extension (\texttt{exp158} Daodejing ---
\textbf{DIRECTIONAL\_F\_UNIVERSAL\_LARGER\_GAP\_FOR\_LOGOGRAPHIC}, 0/3
narrow / 1/3 widened, Tier-C
O13b)}{§4.47.38 --- V3.22: F-Universal logographic-script extension (exp158 Daodejing --- DIRECTIONAL\_F\_UNIVERSAL\_LARGER\_GAP\_FOR\_LOGOGRAPHIC, 0/3 narrow / 1/3 widened, Tier-C O13b)}}\label{v3.22-f-universal-logographic-script-extension-exp158-daodejing-directional_f_universal_larger_gap_for_logographic-03-narrow-13-widened-tier-c-o13b}

V3.18--V3.21 / §4.47.37.1 establish F-Universal
\texttt{H₁\ −\ H\_∞\ ≈\ 1\ b} across \textbf{11 oral canons in 5
unrelated language families --- all using alphabetic / abjad / abugida
scripts}. The next pre-registered question is whether the 1-bit gap
survives extension to a \textbf{logographic} script, where the natural
``verse-final unit'' is a character (morpheme/syllable), not a phoneme.
This addresses the user's HIGH-1 task (Classical Chinese cross-tradition
extension) as the first single-corpus step of the broader CRITICAL-1
N≥50 extension (which remains blocked on data acquisition for the
remaining pool).

\texttt{exp158\_F\_universal\_chinese\_extension} (PREREG hash
\texttt{5d593c51cb8ad54fd187e489d821ec3e65f25e5f21dcae0f211e2d04529e6251},
H103) tests F-Universal on the \textbf{Daodejing} (王弼/Wang Bi
recension, 81 chapters, corpus SHA-256
\texttt{a05c5cb00650263e61d107dbeb7f8b887752bcc82fd42fd286b928d2a4d527bd})
under three plausible ``verse-final unit'' granularities:

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{chapter\_final}: last non-punctuation character of each
  chapter (n = 81)
\item
  \textbf{line\_final}: last non-punctuation character of each
  newline-delimited line within chapters (n = 234)
\item
  \textbf{phrase\_final}: character preceding each Chinese punctuation
  mark (\texttt{。，；：、？！}) within chapters (n = 1 183)
\end{itemize}

\textbf{Pre-registered prediction confirmation}:

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{P1} (≥1 granularity in narrow band): \textbf{FAIL} --- 0/3.
\item
  \textbf{P2} (chapter\_final has smallest gap): \textbf{PASS} ---
  chapter\_final 1.597 \textless{} line\_final 2.659 \textless{}
  phrase\_final 3.986 (strictly monotone).
\item
  \textbf{P3} (phrase\_final has largest gap): \textbf{PASS} --- same
  monotonicity as P2.
\item
  \textbf{P4} (\texttt{H\_∞(chapter\_final)\ ≥\ 3.5\ b}): \textbf{PASS}
  --- observed 4.018 b.
\item
  \textbf{P5} (\texttt{H₁(chapter\_final)\ ≤\ log₂(81)\ =\ 6.34\ b}):
  \textbf{PASS} --- observed 5.615 b.
\end{itemize}

The granularity-monotonicity sanity (C5 audit hook) is satisfied: as the
unit becomes more local (chapter → line → phrase), the gap grows roughly
linearly in \texttt{log(n\_distinct)} --- consistent with finer
granularity sampling longer-tailed distributions. The chapter-final
granularity is the closest analog to ``verse-final letter'' in the
alphabetic 11-corpus pool, but even at this coarsest granularity the gap
exceeds the V3.21 non-Quran-cluster mean by
\texttt{1.597\ −\ 0.943\ =\ 0.654\ b} (≈ 5.6 cluster-standard-errors
above mean) --- clearly outside the F-Universal 1-bit band.

\textbf{Substantive interpretation (post-hoc, NOT a claim)}:
F-Universal's 1-bit gap is \textbf{specific to phonemic-final units in
alphabetic / abjad / abugida scripts} (single-phoneme alphabet of
cardinality A ≈ 25--35). It is \textbf{NOT} a property of canonical
literary corpora in general. The mechanism --- a working-memory channel
where the ``secondary distinction load'' beyond the dominant rhyme
letter is approximately 1 bit (V3.18 §4.47.33.3 cognitive-channel
interpretation) --- assumes the unit space is \textbf{phonemic}, where
each unit is one of \textasciitilde30 letters and the listener's
recognition channel is bounded by Miller-class working memory. In a
logographic script, the unit is a morpheme drawn from a vocabulary of
thousands; the channel reduces to \textbf{chunked-syllable
identification}, where the secondary distinction load is naturally
\texttt{log₂(n\_distinct/p\_max·n\_distinct)\ ≈\ log₂(n\_distinct)}-scale,
not 1-bit-scale. The Daodejing's chapter-final gap of 1.6 b sits
\textbf{closer} to the alphabetic 1-bit signature than to the
uniform-distribution upper bound \texttt{log₂(57)\ =\ 5.83\ b} for that
vocabulary, indicating \textbf{partial concentration} but not the
alphabetic-class compression.

\textbf{What this establishes}:

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  F-Universal is \textbf{scoped to alphabetic-class scripts}, not to
  canonical literary corpora in general. The V3.22 PAPER §4.47.37.1
  statement should be (and now is, per §4.47.37.4 above) read with this
  scope explicitly disclosed.
\item
  The granularity-monotonicity P2 / P3 PASSES validate the experimental
  design: the splitter, entropy computation, and band-check are all
  behaving correctly. The DIRECTIONAL verdict is a \textbf{substantive
  scope-boundary disclosure} at the cross-script level, not a
  methodological artefact.
\item
  \textbf{No locked F75 / F-Universal finding's status changes.} The
  11-corpus N=11 PASS verdict is byte-equivalent to V3.21 and is
  \textbf{explicitly unaffected} by the H103 DIRECTIONAL verdict (per
  audit hook A4 of \texttt{exp158}'s PREREG). F-Universal remains a
  paper-grade Zipf-class universal \textbf{within its alphabetic-script
  scope}.
\end{itemize}

\textbf{What this does not establish}:

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  A claim about Sino-Tibetan family scriptural texts. One corpus
  (Daodejing) is not a family. To establish Sino-Tibetan extension would
  require at minimum the four canonical Confucian-Daoist texts (大學 /
  中庸 / 論語 / 孟子) plus Buddhist Chinese sutras, which are out of
  scope.
\item
  A claim about \textbf{phonemic-transcribed} Daodejing. If the
  Daodejing were romanised under Old Chinese / Middle Chinese / Mandarin
  pinyin reconstructions, the \textbf{letter-final} gap might lie in the
  1-bit band. Such a transcription would prejudge the result and is
  explicitly out of scope (PREREG §7).
\item
  A retraction of the V3.21 / \texttt{exp156} 11-corpus PASS verdict.
  F-Universal at N=11 stands.
\end{itemize}

\textbf{Counts impact (V3.22)}: Tier-C observations 12 → 14 (add
\textbf{O13} for \texttt{exp157} cognitive-channel finite-buffer
directional support, plus \textbf{O13b} for \texttt{exp158}
logographic-script-boundary scope disclosure). Failed-null pre-regs
\textbf{unchanged at 27} (per both PREREGs' counts-impact tables:
PARTIAL and DIRECTIONAL verdicts add Tier-C only, not FN). Retractions
unchanged at 63. RANKED\_FINDINGS row for F75 / F-Universal gains an
explicit ``alphabetic-script scope'' disclosure note.

\subparagraph{§4.47.38.1 --- Honest scope after V3.22 (final
summary)}\label{honest-scope-after-v3.22-final-summary}

V3.22 closes with three coordinated micro-results that together
strengthen F75's theoretical scaffolding \textbf{within its honest
scope} while disclosing its boundary:

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{F-Universal compaction} (§4.47.37.1) --- single-equation
  Rényi-gap form of F75 plus F79 corollary; alias-only, no verdict
  change.
\item
  \textbf{Cognitive-channel finite-buffer support} (§4.47.37.2;
  \texttt{exp157} PARTIAL 3/5) --- central Miller-7 operating point
  recovers β = 1.40 within 0.20 of V3.20 anchor and Route-C regression;
  sensitivity wider than narrow band.
\item
  \textbf{Logographic-script boundary} (§4.47.38; \texttt{exp158}
  DIRECTIONAL 0/3 narrow / 1/3 widened) --- F-Universal does
  \textbf{not} extend to Classical Chinese under any of three plausible
  granularities; the 1-bit gap is alphabetic-script-specific.
\end{enumerate}

Together these define F-Universal's \textbf{scope of validity}:
oral-tradition canons with phonemic-final units in alphabetic / abjad /
abugida scripts, where finite-buffer working-memory MAXENT supports a
Weibull-1.5 cognitive-channel signature. The Quran sits at the rank-1
super-Gaussian extremum of this distribution. Logographic-script canons
(and presumably ideographic-script canons more broadly) lie
\textbf{outside} this universal, evidencing a script-class boundary that
future cross-tradition work would need to characterise quantitatively.

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

  \textbf{Closed-form Rényi-2 derivation of \texttt{EL\_q\ ≈\ 1/√2} from
  \texttt{Σp̂²\ =\ 1/2}} \emph{(new retraction, v7.9 cand., 2026-04-26)}.
  The proposed information-theoretic identity that the Quranic

  Rényi-2 entropy ≈ 1 bit) is \textbf{falsified at the corpus pool}:
  observed \texttt{Σp̂²\ =\ 0.295} (95 \% bootstrap CI {[}0.284,
  0.305{]}; 100 000-bootstrap two-sided p vs the strict band {[}0.495,
  0.505{]} = 0.000), Rényi-2 = 1.763 bits. The mechanism is a
  single-letter dominance: 50.1 \% of verse-finals are \texttt{ن}
  (\texttt{0.501²\ =\ 0.251}). The empirical near-coincidence
  \texttt{EL\_q\ =\ 0.7271\ ≈\ 1/√2\ =\ 0.7071} is preserved as an
  \textbf{average-over-band-A-surahs} identity
  (\texttt{mean\ Σp̂²\ =\ 0.541}, \texttt{√mean\ =\ 0.736}, gap ≈ 4 \%)
  but not as a closed-form pooled-PMF identity. Source:
  \texttt{experiments/expC1plus\_renyi2\_closed\_form/}, verdict
  \texttt{FAIL\_NOT\_HALF}.
\end{itemize}

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\subsection{6. Discussion}\label{discussion}

\subsubsection{6.1 What the data
establish}\label{what-the-data-establish}

The Quran's 5-D band-A fingerprint is a Hotelling TÂ² = 3 557
multivariate outlier vs 2 509 band-A Arabic-family units, perm p â‰¤
1/(N\_PERM+1), nested-CV AUC = 0.998. The effect is robust under
leave-one-family-out (6/6 â‰¥ 1.5 d), 10-fold Quran-internal CV (min
5.26, median 7.30), 1 000-bootstrap Î© (100 \% \textgreater{} 2.0),
replacement of Cohen's d by Hotelling TÂ² (bias-correct), replacement of
\texttt{1\ âˆ’\ chi2.cdf} by \texttt{chi2.sf} (v5), hadith quarantine
(v5), and v6 cross-language fallback removal.

\subsubsection{6.2 What the data do not
establish}\label{what-the-data-do-not-establish}

No universal law. No physics-class constant. No theological inference.
The strongest universal candidate under test --- Î³(Î©) = a + bÂ·Î©
(\texttt{L6}, 7 Arabic corpora) --- returns slope b = âˆ'0.0043,
consistent with zero. The golden-ratio claim does not reproduce. The
only stable numerical constants are H(harakat \textbar{} rasm) and I(EL;
CN) at the corpus level, neither Quran-unique.

\subsubsection{6.3 The ksucca tie on Î©}\label{the-ksucca-tie-on-uxee}

Ksucca ties the Quran on the aggregate Î© (8.43 vs 8.29) but loses under
Î¦\_M (d = 1.43) and loses under the classifier (AUC â‰ˆ 0.998). The
sharpened framing is ``separated even from its nearest Arabic-register
sibling on the multivariate statistic, tied on a specific aggregate
composite.'' Reported prominently, not buried.

\subsubsection{6.4 Benchmarks}\label{benchmarks}

Arabic authorship-attribution AUC benchmarks typically 0.85--0.95
(Mosteller-Wallace class). Particle-physics discovery threshold: 5 Ïƒ (p
â‰ˆ 2.87Â·10â»â·). Raw Mann-Whitney p = 1.75Â·10â»â´â´ exceeds the Higgs
threshold by 37 orders of magnitude in raw z --- but we caveat strongly
that permutation-of-units against sibling Arabic families is a softer
null than the Standard Model background. The \emph{magnitude} is
physics-class; the \emph{null-model rigour} is stylometry-class.

\textbf{Comparative AUC table (added v7.9-cand, 2026-04-26)}:

TDRLM (deep authorship attribution, Twitter--Foursquare) & 0.9247 &

\textbf{0.9932} & 5 & \texttt{expP7}, this paper \\

v7.7 §4.1 \\
\end{longtable}
}

The EL one-feature law on the full Quran (AUC = 0.9813, \textbf{1
feature}) sits 5--7 percentage points above the field-standard
deep-learning authorship-attribution AUCs (0.92--0.93 with hundreds of
embedding features). This is a meaningful margin at the high end of the
AUC scale where ordinary 1-feature stylometric statistics hover near
0.7--0.8.

\textbf{Caveat}: the comparison is across heterogeneous corpora and
tasks; the v7.9-cand result is ``discriminate one specific text from a
heterogeneous Arabic-prose pool,'' not ``attribute one of N candidate
authors.'' A more controlled comparison would be a function-word-PCA
classifier evaluated on the same \texttt{exp104} 4 719-unit Arabic-prose
pool, which has not been done. The honest framing is therefore \emph{``a
1-feature classifier achieves AUC 0.98 on a problem where field-standard
200-feature classifiers achieve 0.85--0.95 on roughly comparable
problems''}, not \emph{``EL beats SOTA''}.

\subsubsection{6.5 Limitations}\label{limitations}

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\tightlist
\item
  Feature-space specificity (partly mitigated by sparse-PCA and kernel
  HSIC robustness).
\item
  External validity: six selected Arabic families; a seventh might close
  the gap.
\item
  Band-A restriction excludes 46 / 114 short or very-long surahs.
\item
  FAST\_MODE N\_PERM = 200 floors perm p at 1/201. A full-mode
  supplementary rerun is \textbf{completed}
  (\texttt{exp26\_perm\_sensitivity}, N = 10 000, p \textless{} 10â»â´,
  0 / 10 000 hits at the observed TÂ²); the abstract and Â§4.1 report
  both values and treat the FAST-mode locked \texttt{4.98\ Ã—\ 10â»Â³}
  as a conservative lower bound on the true p.
\item
  Non-independent sampling within a poetry family.
\item
  CamelTools root-extractor â‰ˆ 63 \% on gold-set; version-pinned.
\item
  Single-author sociological risk; methodology co-author recommended.
\item
  Archived pre-5-D builders (\texttt{build\_pipeline\_p1/p2}) used a
  hard-coded \texttt{VL\_CV\_FLOOR\ =\ 0.1962} with an
  \texttt{\textbar{}}-rule that inflated control separation by +0.36 pp;
  the active 5-D pipeline does not use this logic (Appendix A, item 16;
  \texttt{exp61}).
\end{enumerate}

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\subsection{Appendix A --- Root-cause list for divergence from
v2}\label{appendix-a-root-cause-list-for-divergence-from-v2}

Six drivers closed in the v5--v6 cycle, plus one closure and three new
items in v7:

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{Hadith leakage (V2)} --- hadith\_bukhari quarantined from
  controls; new \texttt{Partial\_quote\_leak\ =\ 0.008}.
\item
  \textbf{Band-A filter propagation (V3)} --- previously not applied to
  T1 (clean\_pipeline) and T8 (extended\_tests); corrected.
\item
  \textbf{Fisher 1âˆ'CDF â†' chi2.sf (V4)} --- machine-epsilon floor at
  W = 10 replaced with genuine \texttt{chi2.sf}; \texttt{D07} now 16.08,
  log-domain reblessed.
\item
  \textbf{Ridge unified at 1Â·10â»â¶ (V4)} --- multiple discrepant ridge
  values across Hotelling / HSIC paths unified.
\item
  \textbf{D07 bless as âˆ'logâ‚â‚€ p (V4)} --- raw p bottomed out at
  10â»Â¹â¶; now blessed in the log domain.
\item
  \textbf{Cross-language fallback removed (v6-W2)} --- silent
  \texttt{recs\ =\ FEATS{[}cl{]}} substitution when band-A was empty
  replaced with INFEASIBLE skip.
\item
  \textbf{v7-W1 Cross-language closed at the proper per-scripture null}
  --- the v6 INFEASIBLE skip for Iliad/Greek-NT/Tanakh is resolved by R3
  (Â§4.16) using a within-scripture book-shuffle null rather than a
  forced band-A match. BH-pooled p = 0.002.
\item
  \textbf{v7-W2 Adiyat letter-level ceiling reframed} --- the Î¦\_M 2--3
  \% ceiling on single-letter edits was reported in v3--v6 as a
  \emph{system} ceiling; in v7 it is a Î¦\_M-specific ceiling only. R2
  sliding-window amplification achieves a median 23Ã--- enhancement of
  the same edit signal at 10-verse resolution (Â§4.14).
\item
  \textbf{v7-W3 Hostile-audit discipline formalised} --- Ultimate-2
  required two adversarial audit rounds before bless (13 + 5 FATAL, 21 +
  8 WARN). The resulting audit protocol is now the standing acceptance
  criterion for any future R-channel addition (any R12+). Audit logs:
  \texttt{archive/audits/}.
\item
  \textbf{v7.1-W1 Scale-invariant universal-law framing audited} --- the
  external-review claim that the Quran is Markov-1-extremal at every
  scale simultaneously is falsified at 2 of 5 tested scales (Â§4.19,
  verdict \texttt{PARTIAL\_LAW\_HOLDS\_AT\_MAJORITY\_SCALES}). The 3
  surviving scales are retained as independent findings; the uniform law
  claim is retracted (Â§5). Driver:
  \texttt{experiments/exp27\_hchar\_bigram/},
  \texttt{experiments/exp28\_scale\_invariant\_law/}.
\item
  \textbf{v7.1-W2 Cascade product-code framing reframed} --- the
  external-review claim that single-letter internal substitutions are
  detectable via a cascade of independent channels with composite P =
  0.82--0.90 is empirically falsified: measured P\_composite = 0.137
  (Â§4.20). Three of four channels are structurally blind to
  internal-letter edits because \texttt{features\_5d} is byte-exact
  invariant under those edits; this is a mathematical property, not a
  precision issue. Corpus-level separation (Â§4.1) is unaffected.
  Driver: \texttt{experiments/exp29\_cascade\_product\_code/}.
\item
  \textbf{v7.1-W3 T28 root-Markov-order sign-flip surfaced} ---
  \texttt{T28\_markov\_order.cohens\_d\_quran\_vs\_ctrl\ =\ +0.425} is
  the observed direction in the locked
  \texttt{CLEAN\_PIPELINE\_REPORT.json}; the T28 docstring's
  \texttt{d\ =\ âˆ’1.849} is therefore a pre-existing mis-statement
  attached to a correct scalar. The scalar is not modified. Verbal claim
  retracted in Â§5. Driver:
  \texttt{experiments/exp28\_scale\_invariant\_law/}.
\item
  \textbf{v7.2-W1 R3 cross-scripture rebuild} --- the v7.1 Â§4.16 table
  inherited
  \texttt{z\_Quran\ =\ âˆ’8.74,\ z\_GreekNT\ =\ âˆ’4.97,\ z\_Tanakh\ =\ âˆ’5.02}
  from the v10.3c \texttt{qsf\_breakthrough\_tests.py} pipeline that was
  deleted in the v3â†'v5 cleanup; \texttt{integrity/corpus\_lock.json}
  had Hebrew Tanakh and Greek NT marked \texttt{exists\ =\ false} at
  obsolete paths. The actual corpora
  (\texttt{data/corpora/he/tanakh\_wlc.txt},
  \texttt{data/corpora/el/opengnt\_v3\_3.csv}) are on disk, and
  \texttt{raw\_loader.py} supports them via
  \texttt{include\_cross\_lang\ =\ True}. A fresh v7.2 run
  (\texttt{exp35\_R3\_cross\_scripture\_redo}, N\_PERM = 5 000 per
  scripture) gives
  \texttt{z\_Quran\ =\ âˆ’8.92,\ z\_Tanakh\ =\ âˆ’15.29,\ z\_GreekNT\ =\ âˆ’12.06,\ z\_Iliad\ =\ +0.34},
  supersedes the v7.1 table, and FALSIFIES the ``Quran â‰ˆ76 \% stronger
  than next scripture'' framing (see Â§5 row for detail).
\item
  \textbf{v7.2-W2 Integrity locks refreshed} ---
  \texttt{results/integrity/corpus\_lock.json} had 6 of 10 entries
  marked \texttt{exists\ =\ false} at never-used paths (pre-v3 typos).
  The lock is refreshed against the actual on-disk set (11 corpora:
  quran\_bare, quran\_vocal, tashkeela, arabic\_bible.xlsx, hadith.json,
  hindawi, ksucca, poetry\_raw.csv, hebrew\_tanakh\_wlc,
  iliad\_perseus.xml, opengnt\_v3\_3.csv).
  \texttt{results/integrity/code\_lock.json} now includes
  \texttt{src/cache/cameltools\_root\_cache.pkl.gz} (SHA
  \texttt{82b24d12…}), which was the last un-pinned contributor to Î¦\_M
  reproducibility. \texttt{requirements.txt} pins
  \texttt{camel-tools==1.5.7} exactly (replacing a commented-out
  \texttt{\textgreater{}=1.5.0}). Effect: the reproducibility surface is
  now fully SHA-pinned end-to-end.
\item
  **v7.2-W3 Robustness / topology / meta-CI / Adiyat-Î¦\_sym additions**
  --- Â§Â§4.21--4.24 add four measurements that were implicit reviewer
  gaps: subset-centroid stationarity (exp31), 5-D topological character
  of the separation (exp33, silhouette = +0.65 under a continuum null),
  (T, EL) AUC meta-CI across 5 seeds (exp36, Ïƒ across seeds =
  5.6Â·10â»â´), and Î¦\_sym applied to the Adiyat variants (exp34,
  structural blindness confirmed). None of these changes a locked
  scalar; they close standing objections.
\item
  \textbf{v7.6-W1 Legacy 8-D VL\_CV\_FLOOR = 0.1962 audited as
  methodological leak (exp61)} --- the pre-5-D
  \texttt{build\_pipeline\_p1.py} (archived) used a hard-coded
  \texttt{VL\_CV\_FLOOR\ =\ 0.1962} together with the rule
  \texttt{c\_out\ =\ (d\_M\ \textgreater{}\ Ï„)\ \textbar{}\ floor\_excluded},
  auto-classifying any Band-A control with
  \texttt{VL\_CV\ \textless{}\ 0.1962} as ``correctly separated''
  without a distance test. Because the 68 Band-A Quran units all have
  \texttt{VL\_CV\ â‰¥\ 0.268} (Quran min), only the Arabic control pool
  was ever floor-excluded. \texttt{exp61\_vl\_cv\_floor\_sensitivity}
  quantified the artefact: \textbf{the constant has no principled
  derivation} --- closest math formula \texttt{1/(Ï†Â·Ï€)\ =\ 0.19673}
  off by Î'' = 5.3Â·10â»â´ (outside the 5Â·10â»â´ rounding-precision
  tolerance); closest clean percentile off by Î'' = 2.55Â·10â»Â³
  (outside the 2Â·10â»Â³ finite-sample tolerance); actual value
  corresponds to the \textbf{56.88th percentile} of the 2 509-unit
  Arabic-control VL\_CV distribution, i.e.~an empirical overfit to the
  control pool. Under the legacy OR-rule this inflated reported control
  separation by \textbf{+0.36 pp} (sep rises 0.9777 â†' 0.9813 at Ï„* =
  Quran d\_M p5) and lifted full-sample Mahalanobis AUC by
  \textbf{+1.1Â·10â»Â³} (0.9947 â†' 0.9959) --- a small but directional
  bias, always control-favorable because Quran never triggers the floor.
  \textbf{Stability of the underlying ranking}: with the floor stripped,
  AUC varies by only 5.2Â·10â»Â³ across \texttt{f\ âˆˆ\ {[}0,\ 0.25{]}}
  (well below the 10â»Â² stability threshold), confirming the 5-D
  Mahalanobis fingerprint does not need the floor. \textbf{The active
  5-D pipeline (\texttt{src/clean\_pipeline.py}, all phase checkpoints)
  does NOT use this floor} and is therefore unaffected; locked scalars
  in \texttt{results/results\_lock.json} (Phi\_M\_hotelling\_T2 = 3 557,
  nested-CV AUC, etc.) were generated post-refactor and do not carry the
  inflation. Entry recorded for methodological transparency against any
  reader returning to the archived legacy code. Driver:
  \texttt{experiments/exp61\_vl\_cv\_floor\_sensitivity/}.
\end{enumerate}

Deprecations are documented in \texttt{src/extended\_tests*.py} and
cross-referenced in \texttt{results/integrity/results\_lock.json}.
Ultimate-2 deprecations (Law IV, R9 direction, R5 G4 framing) are logged
in Â§5. v7.1 retractions (char-scale bigram sufficiency, scale-invariant
universal-law, char-root GAP, T28 sign, cascade composite, Adiyat
Ø¹â†'Øº-specific) are also logged in Â§5. **v7.2 adds the R3 v10.3c
falsification and the Î¦\_sym / Adiyat-variant structural-blindness
disclosure. v7.6 adds the archived-legacy VL\_CV\_FLOOR = 0.1962
methodological-leak disclosure (item 16, \texttt{exp61}), with no effect
on any active locked scalar.**
